\t\t\t\u003C!-- #BeginEditable \"headlinenews\" -->\n    \n        \n            \u003Cdiv class=\"messagebox announcement\">\n                \u003Cp>When submitting comments on planning applications, be aware that they will be made available online. Personal details such as telephone numbers and email addresses will be redacted, but your name and address will still be visible. Therefore, avoid including any personal information that you wouldn't want to be public.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If your comment exceeds 2000 characters, submit additional comments online and start the new comment with \"Continued\". Comments submitted after the statutory consultation deadline but before a decision is made may still be considered. If you wish to submit comments after the deadline, you should email them to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk. Be sure to include the application number in the subject line and clearly indicate whether you are objecting, supporting, or simply commenting on the application.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If you prefer not to have your name and address published online, you can email your comment to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk, explicitly stating that you do not want your details to be published online. Ensure that you include the application number and the address to which your comment pertains. While your name and address will not be proactively published, they might still be disclosed in response to an EIR request, subject to a public interest test.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>For additional help, you can contact the planning office by phone at 020 8359 3000, available from 9 AM to 5 PM, Monday to Friday.\u003C/p>\n            \u003C/div>\n        \n    \n\u003C!-- #EndEditable -->\n\n \t\t\t\u003C!-- #BeginEditable \"headlinenews\" -->\n    \n        \n            \u003Cdiv class=\"messagebox announcement\">\n                \u003Cp>When submitting comments on planning applications, be aware that they will be made available online. Personal details such as telephone numbers and email addresses will be redacted, but your name and address will still be visible. Therefore, avoid including any personal information that you wouldn't want to be public.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If your comment exceeds 2000 characters, submit additional comments online and start the new comment with \"Continued\". Comments submitted after the statutory consultation deadline but before a decision is made may still be considered. If you wish to submit comments after the deadline, you should email them to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk. Be sure to include the application number in the subject line and clearly indicate whether you are objecting, supporting, or simply commenting on the application.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If you prefer not to have your name and address published online, you can email your comment to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk, explicitly stating that you do not want your details to be published online. Ensure that you include the application number and the address to which your comment pertains. While your name and address will not be proactively published, they might still be disclosed in response to an EIR request, subject to a public interest test.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>For additional help, you can contact the planning office by phone at 020 8359 3000, available from 9 AM to 5 PM, Monday to Friday.\u003C/p>\n            \u003C/div>\n        \n    \n\u003C!-- #EndEditable -->\n\n \t\t\t\u003C!-- #BeginEditable \"headlinenews\" -->\n    \n        \n            \u003Cdiv class=\"messagebox announcement\">\n                \u003Cp>When submitting comments on planning applications, be aware that they will be made available online. Personal details such as telephone numbers and email addresses will be redacted, but your name and address will still be visible. Therefore, avoid including any personal information that you wouldn't want to be public.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If your comment exceeds 2000 characters, submit additional comments online and start the new comment with \"Continued\". Comments submitted after the statutory consultation deadline but before a decision is made may still be considered. If you wish to submit comments after the deadline, you should email them to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk. Be sure to include the application number in the subject line and clearly indicate whether you are objecting, supporting, or simply commenting on the application.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If you prefer not to have your name and address published online, you can email your comment to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk, explicitly stating that you do not want your details to be published online. Ensure that you include the application number and the address to which your comment pertains. While your name and address will not be proactively published, they might still be disclosed in response to an EIR request, subject to a public interest test.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>For additional help, you can contact the planning office by phone at 020 8359 3000, available from 9 AM to 5 PM, Monday to Friday.\u003C/p>\n            \u003C/div>\n        \n    \n\u003C!-- #EndEditable -->\n\n \t\t\t\u003C!-- #BeginEditable \"headlinenews\" -->\n    \n        \n            \u003Cdiv class=\"messagebox announcement\">\n                \u003Cp>When submitting comments on planning applications, be aware that they will be made available online. Personal details such as telephone numbers and email addresses will be redacted, but your name and address will still be visible. Therefore, avoid including any personal information that you wouldn't want to be public.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If your comment exceeds 2000 characters, submit additional comments online and start the new comment with \"Continued\". Comments submitted after the statutory consultation deadline but before a decision is made may still be considered. If you wish to submit comments after the deadline, you should email them to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk. Be sure to include the application number in the subject line and clearly indicate whether you are objecting, supporting, or simply commenting on the application.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If you prefer not to have your name and address published online, you can email your comment to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk, explicitly stating that you do not want your details to be published online. Ensure that you include the application number and the address to which your comment pertains. While your name and address will not be proactively published, they might still be disclosed in response to an EIR request, subject to a public interest test.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>For additional help, you can contact the planning office by phone at 020 8359 3000, available from 9 AM to 5 PM, Monday to Friday.\u003C/p>\n            \u003C/div>\n        \n    \n\u003C!-- #EndEditable -->\n\n \t\t\t\u003C!-- #BeginEditable \"headlinenews\" -->\n    \n        \n            \u003Cdiv class=\"messagebox announcement\">\n                \u003Cp>When submitting comments on planning applications, be aware that they will be made available online. Personal details such as telephone numbers and email addresses will be redacted, but your name and address will still be visible. Therefore, avoid including any personal information that you wouldn't want to be public.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If your comment exceeds 2000 characters, submit additional comments online and start the new comment with \"Continued\". Comments submitted after the statutory consultation deadline but before a decision is made may still be considered. If you wish to submit comments after the deadline, you should email them to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk. Be sure to include the application number in the subject line and clearly indicate whether you are objecting, supporting, or simply commenting on the application.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>If you prefer not to have your name and address published online, you can email your comment to planning.consultation@barnet.gov.uk, explicitly stating that you do not want your details to be published online. Ensure that you include the application number and the address to which your comment pertains. While your name and address will not be proactively published, they might still be disclosed in response to an EIR request, subject to a public interest test.\u003C/p>\n\n\u003Cp>For additional help, you can contact the planning office by phone at 020 8359 3000, available from 9 AM to 5 PM, Monday to Friday.\u003C/p>\n            \u003C/div>\n        \n    \n\u003C!-- #EndEditable -->\n\n
